# A Local’s Guide to Where to Stay in San Francisco: Best Boutique Hotels

November 8, 2025

Last updated on April 27th, 2026 at 09:30 pm

Hey MTV, welcome to my crib!!!!! Okay, you’re not MTV, but you _are_ here to figure out where to stay in San Francisco, right? Whether you’re here for the Golden Gate Bridge or to drive around in a robot car, you’re probably wondering where to stay in San Francisco that actually feels like the real city and not a tourist trap.

Look, I know San Francisco gets a bad rap these days, but let me set the record straight — this city is absolutely **_stunning_.** I personally grew up in the Bay Area and have lived in San Francisco for the last decade. Yet, I continue to be obsessed with our pastel-colored Victorians, the cable cars chugging along California street, and the views of the [Golden Gate bridge](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a1063%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=6rLaWsPAfIOxEGX0PCeJg&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) at sunset from [Crissy Field](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D259159%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=AAUjjWec6KB2_Eq8nZxkW&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). If you ignore the overly negative image the media loves to push, then you’ll soon understand why **thousands** of people fall head over heels for SF every year 🌁

Yes, just like any major city, we have our rough areas, but the “doomloop” headlines don’t tell the full story. **The reality?** We’re a buzzing, innovative city with some of the cutest boutique hotels and the most charming neighborhoods. So trust me, you’ll have plenty of great options when deciding where to stay in San Francisco.

In this guide, I’ll break down the best neighborhoods in San Francisco for a safe and enjoyable stay. From waterfront hotels along [The Embarcadero](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a8932%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=ZaH2I8D23gwiHPacJt_nD&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) to design-forward stays in The Marina, I’ve got all the information for **where to stay in San Francisco for first time visitors.** Plus, a handpicked selection on alllllll the cutest and dreamiest boutique hotels. Lastly, I’ve also included a quick FAQ at the bottom to answer all your burning questions about _the city by the bay._

**Why should you trust me?** Well, I grew up here and currently live in Nob Hill. So I can guarantee that I’ve got the most up-to-date, no-BS take on where to stay for a safe, stress-free visit to [San Francisco](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fsan-francisco-l61%2F&trs=299090&journey_id=XKCmZ6Qp-fcRREH7SQ11z&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") 🌉

## Breakdown of San Francisco Neighborhoods

![](https://i.imgur.com/MPZSeYX.jpeg)

[San Francisco](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=594&marker=522542&p=8645&trs=299090&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.expedia.com%2FHotel-Search%3Fadults%3D2%26afflid%3D1100lAdhTYT4%26clickref%3D1100lAdhTYT4%26my_ad%3DAFF.US.DIRECT.PHG.1011l45458.0%26numRoom%3D1%26ref_id%3D1100lAdhTYT4%26regionId%3D3132&product_type=linkswitcher&journey_id=RFbJtnwQKfK7h3wAWATED&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&install_type=partner ""), located on the northern tip of California’s San Francisco Peninsula, is a vibrant city known for its stunning views, classic landmarks, and rich history. Spanning just 7 miles by 7 miles, it’s also one of the most compact major cities in the U.S.

Ps. SF is literally nicknamed [7×7](https://www.7x7.com/ "") because of how small our city dimensions are.

San Francisco’s neighborhoods are as diverse as the people who live here, and trust me, there’s a spot for everyone. The Marina and [Pacific Heights](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1433%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=xcwRkP0LEZYE1LyrmMDzw&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) are your go-to for stunning views and chic dining, while [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1436%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=vqLi7AH4bukLNlOunYVh5&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) and [Russian Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1430%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=Q6FAtvZmEUilRNtmMKs0z&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) serve up a little old-school charm with those iconic, sweeping panoramas. And hills 🥵

If you’re in the mood for classic tourist fun, head over to [Fisherman’s Wharf](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1432%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=7Ond23o16OtF3ZAVzdnXr&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) for seafood, shopping, and all the sights. [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=sWkypo0sXUubxnTltNZ7V&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F)’s got your back for shopping and art, while the Financial District (FiDi) pulses with business energy.

[Richmond](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D20141027%26dest_type%3Dcity&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=hYiIiv5ScmdV9v3LlndkT&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) and Sunset? A quieter, more laid-back vibe with cozy restaurants and parks to relax in. Many of these neighborhoods fall under the safest areas in San Francisco to stay, making your visit both fun and worry-free. Whether you’re looking for charm, views, or convenience, the safest areas in San Francisco to stay offer something for every kind of traveler. So stick with me, and I’ll take you through each one — neighborhood by neighborhood!

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: The Marina

![](https://i.imgur.com/LK7eeEX.jpeg)

I know, I know. Every guidebook and travel blog will probably tell you to stay in [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=3H2NtcPOk8q6Wfj5ZwwW7&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). But let me let you in on a little secret: the [Marina District](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1774%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=J0FG35IKWD6Xxy0eJFUTa&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is where it’s _really_ at.

I actually lived here for over five years before my fiancé and I made the move to [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1436%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=4JsQ7lvKlupWqnugFnkwl&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), so I’m speaking from experience when I say it’s hands down the best neighborhood in San Francisco.

From stunning views of the [Golden Gate](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fsan-francisco-l61%2F&trs=299090&journey_id=uJhs2g9c2NerVNYuGiAuk&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") to charming boutiques, fitness studios, and top-notch dining, it’s got the perfect mix of everything.

Plus, it’s one of the safest areas in San Francisco to stay. Whether you’re walking around at night or grabbing coffee in the morning, you’ll feel totally at ease. The safest areas when deciding where to stay in San Francisco aren’t just secure, they’re also full of character. The Marina is a perfect example, with charm, walkability, and classic SF vibes.

Trust me, if you’re looking for a spot to stay that’s both lively and secure, the Marina’s got you covered.

### Things to do in the Marina

![](https://i.imgur.com/jNedsSH.jpeg)

There’s so much to do in The Marina but I’d say the main things are to…

- Hit the parks and hangout on the lawns of Crissy Field, Marina Green, Presidio Tunnel Tops, and Fort Mason
- Go shopping on both Chestnut and Union Street
- Take in the epic views of the Golden Gate Bridge from [a cruise along the ocean](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fsan-francisco-l61%2F&trs=299090&journey_id=s7tomgXpNsM2kT-oU4iDw&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner ""), Fort Point National Historic Site, and/or the Golden Gate Overlook
- Dine at top-rated restaurants like [Little Original Joe’s](https://www.littleoriginaljoes.com/ ""), [Mamanoko](https://www.mamanokosf.com/ ""), and more.
- Sip on handcrafted cocktails from Left Door (where we had our wedding reception), Wilder, and Balboa Café (known for their famous espressotinis)

Ps. For a complete list of my favorite eats, [head to my local’s guide on how to spend 3 perfect days in San Francisco!](https://discoveroverthere.com/3-day-san-francisco-itinerary/ "")

The Marina has plenty to do, but more importantly, **this is where the locals actually hang out.**

**Main Takeaway:** [The Marina](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D76711%26dest_type%3Dhotel&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=a5jR-IbwPGoyanusocSZ9&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is not only one of San Francisco’s trendiest neighborhoods but also one of the safest areas in San Francisco to stay. Stay here for charming coffee shops, great shopping, epic [Golden Gate Bridge](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a1063%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=HAlwNc4jfoxHkzElL6G8p&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) views, and easy access to Marin and Sausalito. It’s also one of the safest picks when deciding where to stay in San Francisco, especially for solo travelers.

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: Union Square

![](https://i.imgur.com/u9XsLPs.jpeg)

Okay well obviously I’m going to talk about Union Square next since it’s a great location for a wide range of hotel types. [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=2PLSI4eLo8m_HQVLWDV5l&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is basically the go-to spot for first-time visitors, and honestly, I get why. It’s packed with hotels, nonstop shopping, cocktail bars, theaters, and some of the best restaurants in the city.

During the day, you can hop from designer boutiques to local shops, and by night, the area is buzzing with rooftop bars, craft cocktail spots, and top-tier dining. Plus, it’s a major transit hub, so getting around the city is a breeze. It’s also generally safe. Yes it’s _technically_ a neighboring area to the [Tenderloin](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D2128%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=3_86HWet3QADoxsK-HFEb&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) which is the “sketchy” part of town but you’ll be completely fine in the center of Union Square.

In the FAQ section below, I’ll give you exactly which streets and areas to avoid in San Francisco. But believe me, [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=d_hcVMfXBYpEicJqPedpg&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is **NOT** one of them!

If you want to be in the middle of all the action with everything at your doorstep, [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=26s4nSV0gBmk65eX5CRiT&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is a solid choice.

### Things to do in Union Square

![](https://i.imgur.com/VdP6KLt.jpeg)

Since [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=pqJwZ4RrIQ-bPt9FfwzhC&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is San Francisco’s shopping, dining, and entertainment scene — that means it’s pretty much always packed with things to do year-round.

You’ll want to take some photos at the Dewey Monument and heart sculptures, then explore high-end boutiques, department stores, and local shops lining the square. Don’t miss the San Francisco cable car turnaround at the end of Powell Street, where you can hop on a $8 historic ride up to [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a9269%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=dGdO1YDTegjFo_jqK9N_p&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) or [Fisherman’s Wharf](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a1061%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=SUHPzXsPToK_3XQPABMad&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F).

If you’re in SF during the holidays, you _have_ to check out the [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=TCoIFwOVtrHgU_61LSACd&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) ice rink. The whole square transforms into a festive wonderland with a giant skating rink and an even bigger Christmas tree. Oh, and they recently added [Let’s Glow SF](https://downtownsf.org/things-to-do/lets-glow-sf ""), a pretty cool light show that projects massive art displays onto downtown buildings every night during the holiday season.

One of the best things you can do is hit up a [food tour in Chinatown](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fsan-francisco-l61%2Fculinary-walking-tour-of-chinatown-t9463%2F%3Franking_uuid%3Dde6453b4-a42f-4f5b-a3a7-e47f0cd293cb&trs=299090&journey_id=w8lWTDr0flVRnjejc7WDh&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner ""). It’s so close and totally worth it. I always tell my friends visiting for the first time to check out [this particular one](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fsan-francisco-l61%2Fculinary-walking-tour-of-chinatown-t9463%2F%3Franking_uuid%3Dde6453b4-a42f-4f5b-a3a7-e47f0cd293cb&trs=299090&journey_id=bpYP6PYYLMYUakuajeX1L&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") because I think they stop at all the best places. Like the Golden Gate Fortune Cookie Factory 🥠🥠🥠

For my favorite hidden gem, head inside the recently renovated [Westin St. Francis](https://tripadvisor.tpk.lu/kp0OZDNV?trs=299090&journey_id=nU3YF2V-MeOYHSBToh0TC&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_short&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") and check out the [Chateau Montelena Tasting Room](http://e/ ""), where you can sip world-class Napa Valley wines without ever leaving the city.

**Main Takeaway:** If you want to be in the heart of San Francisco’s action, [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=2xCTyWYww0wDUIRdae_uI&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is the place to stay. With endless shopping, top-tier restaurants, and easy access to public transit (including the iconic cable cars), it’s a prime spot for first-time visitors.

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: Nob Hill

![](https://i.imgur.com/b3W9VJr.jpeg)

Alright, you might start to think this article’s a little biased towards neighborhoods I’ve lived in or currently live in…and you’d be right!

But hey, I like to live in nice, clean, and safe parts of San Francisco, which is exactly why I’m all about Nob Hill.

Whether it’s your first time or your 7th time visiting, this neighborhood is perfect for anyone who wants a blend of history, charm, and luxury. Or for anyone who enjoys getting their a\*\* kicked by all of the crazy hills.

My favorite part about [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1436%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=hWEo5et01qoiyQpXmNhcU&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is that you’ll get stunning views of the city, plus a mix of high-end hotels, cozy cafes, underrated Italian restaurants, and historic landmarks like [Grace Cathedral](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a1066%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=A5Y_tI9XfVHIm3a8sCiz7&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), The Masonic, [The Cable Car Museum](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a23209%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=w2Lm2o-5MWRRGSXMUzIKE&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), and [Huntington Park](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a20981%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=12u0q9ww7abPha77t7rym&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). Which just happens to be where you’ll find my dog and I almost every evening after work 🐶

It’s peaceful, central, and hands down one of the best places to stay in SF.

So yeah, maybe I’m a little biased, but [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1436%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=pAoBNEkPkgUnw567koF11&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) really does have it all 😺

### Things to do in Nob Hill

![](https://i.imgur.com/cGPUb90.jpeg)

I mentioned some of the best things to do in [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1436%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=9MDIVS-rAPYNIXamy_M2d&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) already but definitely want to hi-light both Grace Cathedral and [The Cable Car Museum](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a23209%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=sgVGKwwwVtJ1nCf9gnrz0&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). [Grace Cathedral](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a1066%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=AOj7KKd-y05Hf9dLt4K0t&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is a stunning Gothic-style cathedral known for its beautiful stained glass, labyrinth walks, and breathtaking interior. Sometimes they even hold “yoga by candlelight” inside the church and it’s seriously a transformational experience.

Then there’s [The Cable Car Museum](https://www.cablecarmuseum.org/ "") which is kinda quirky but I love it. It’s definitely a must-visit for history buffs (like myself) as it gives you a behind-the-scenes look at how SF’s cable cars work. Spoiler: they’re manual AF and I never know how the workers do it for 8+ hours a day.

As for restaurants and dining, there’s **SO MANY** good hidden gems. There’s [Nob Hill Cafe](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=4456&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FRestaurant_Review-g60713-d353941-Reviews-Nob_Hill_Cafe-San_Francisco_California.html&trs=299090&journey_id=GBMo6IvwRqgT1MdOW7Zw7&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") which is an iconic Italian restaurant, [Key Klub](https://www.keyklubsf.com/ "") which serves natural wine, and [Liholiho Yacht Club](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=4456&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FRestaurant_Review-g60713-d7627146-Reviews-Liholiho_Yacht_Club-San_Francisco_California.html&trs=299090&journey_id=U9whLfiTuyDIfWHAgfeES&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner ""). Where aloha meets San Francisco at this popular dinner spot that serves Hawaiian, Californian, and Asian-inspired dishes. 🍙

_Ps. If you’re craving a bomb burrito but don’t feel like making the trek to the [Mission District](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Ftours%2FSan-Francisco%2FSmall-Group-Mission-District-Food-Tour-San-Francisco%2Fd651-7812P13%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=aSqVHbWIgKkdXVEFQYwpQ&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), head to El Super Burrito on Polk Street in [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a9269%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=m9Y4HluPsqVsnVq-rfGsX&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). It’s a total hidden gem. Known for its massive portions and authentic flavors, this spot will satisfy your burrito cravings without the tourists 🌯_

**Main Takeaway**: [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1436%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=FtvezBsPjaZqPFuxWLPzG&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is where history, luxury, and stunning views come together. If you want a **safe,** elegant neighborhood with renowned hotels, classic San Francisco charm, and easy access to the rest of the city, this is the place to stay.

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: Russian Hill

![](https://i.imgur.com/wpDDSZa.jpeg)

Just down the hill from [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1436%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=Asw0L1yrKYBr__Q4H-Svb&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) (and up another — because, well, welcome to San Francisco), [Russian Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1430%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=L6BlCxutACKirHAXGuubF&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is a mostly residential neighborhood packed with scenic streets, charming cafes, and, of course, the iconic [Lombard Street](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17256%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=IWqKa8p761sNAZF0DE_sF&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), aka the world’s most famous crooked road.

If you’re deciding where to stay in San Francisco and want classic city charm with a quieter feel, this area is a gem.

### Things to do in Russian Hill

![](https://i.imgur.com/x0a79BH.jpeg)

Given that it’s mostly a residential area, there’s not a ton of major attractions besides [Lombard Street](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17256%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=BjVmPComINh6Pk7Lkj3gN&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). Which is why you know that it’s definitely a safe place to stay since a lot of locals live nearby. However, there’s Francisco Park, which is a huge bi-level park that overlooks the bay, that’s worth checking out.

There’s also some of my favorite places to eat such as [Elephant Sushi](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=4456&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FRestaurant_Review-g60713-d6533570-Reviews-Elephant_Sushi-San_Francisco_California.html&trs=299090&journey_id=rlye-yi24D2C4tiJ9Z78f&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner ""), [Seven Hills](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=4456&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FRestaurant_Review-g60713-d1999071-Reviews-Seven_Hills-San_Francisco_California.html&trs=299090&journey_id=ik2g6Gga9fVfrSYyRgw1D&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner ""), [Saru Handroll Bar](https://www.yelp.com/biz/saru-handroll-bar-san-francisco-2 ""), and [Leopold’s.](https://www.yelp.com/biz/leopolds-san-francisco-2 "") You also can’t miss [Swensen’s](https://swensensofsf.com/ "") for a sweet treat after dinner 🍦

**Main Takeaway**: [Russian Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1430%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=glze1mfr8iIjnYm0kU836&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is one of the safest areas in San Francisco to stay, with classic charm, stunning views, quiet residential streets, and easy access to [Lombard Street](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17256%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=yG_sfQ4jQMzsC0IOfnSb5&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), [North Beach](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1435%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=r9FMxgtkd8Ezmal9Q7Iev&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), and the waterfront. If you’re figuring out where to stay in San Francisco and want somewhere walkable, charming, and super local, this area is one of the safest and best choices.

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: Pacific Heights (Pac Heights)

![](https://i.imgur.com/Ke0fExJ.jpeg)

Alright, I promise. This is the last of the hills. [Pacific Heights](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1433%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=d4aco5Y6dHKrkr_LRwsgx&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) aka Pac Heights is one of SF’s most picturesque (and upscale) neighborhoods, stretching from the edge of [Japantown](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1440%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=WnNUew-Qb8SNv1MP2gVeg&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) all the way down to the [Richmond District](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1424%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=zAM2L3flFaPngffGhGk5n&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F).

Think grand mansions, tree-lined streets, and some of the best views in the city. Especially from Lafayette Park (my dog’s 2nd home) and the famous [Lyon Street Steps](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Ftours%2FSan-Francisco%2FHidden-Stairways-of-San-Francisco%2Fd651-74127P3%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=Ty5Vh1TxOBj_tha6_hj9g&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F).

While it’s mostly residential, it’s home to some fantastic boutique shopping and dining along [Fillmore Street](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a8925%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=GoO0ZPA3FyHL4mvQNAe1L&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), plus it puts you within easy reach of both downtown and the quieter western neighborhoods.

If you want a beautiful, safe, and peaceful place to stay with a mix of historic charm and local vibes, [Pacific Heights](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1433%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=UB7JBA2vHsGA74oUFrABo&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is a solid choice.

### Things to do in Pacific Heights (Pac Heights)

![](https://i.imgur.com/6R7mtz1.jpeg)

Since [Pac Heights](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a22020%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=B9_euED6Pc83DurmMgknM&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is pretty spread out, I’d suggest spending more time near [Japantown](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a17277%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=GhzNEdCaXGBIfr2j6VpUO&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) and closer to [Fillmore Street](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a8925%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=bItyoy9PWUPT1iXOYK7Bu&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). The rest is mostly residential.

You can take a stroll through Lafayette Park for some of the best views of the [Golden Gate Bridge](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a1063%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=34aZJtn8FscBHiM17wtPf&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) and [San Francisco Bay](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a8933%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=Dl4KuwX4yu-zd1la_fXgv&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), or explore the beautiful [Alamo Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D5927%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=tamkb6eCR9BPVuIAT2jqh&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) for classic photo ops with the famous [Painted Ladies](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17266%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=rmj_vkhmvQawkxv6hShx2&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F).

For shopping and dining, you’ll want to head down to Fillmore Street. It’s a big, long street filled with a mix of brand names (Lululemon, Sezane, Kiehl’s, etc) and smaller boutiques. My favorite places to eat/drink on Fillmore are [The Tailor’s Son](https://www.thetailorssonsf.com/ ""), [The Snug](https://www.thesnugsf.com/ ""), and [State Bird Provisions](https://www.statebirdsf.com/ "") (super casual 1 Michelin Star restaurant).

You can check out my full review of [The Tailor’s Son](https://discoveroverthere.com/10-exceptional-italian-restaurants-in-san-francisco/ "") in my list of [Top 10 Italian restaurants in San Francisco!](https://discoveroverthere.com/10-exceptional-italian-restaurants-in-san-francisco/ "")

**Main Takeaway**: I’d say staying in [Pac Heights](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D2749403%26dest_type%3Dhotel&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=9c0VFRXDELFJf94hmM_ax&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is pretty similar to staying in [Russian Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1430%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=5Z_bDzbtjYFFjfYtL9dzy&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). It’s safe, peaceful, and more upscale with easy access to some notable sights, beautiful parks, and boutique shops.

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: Fisherman’s Wharf

![](https://i.imgur.com/tWfsQsG.jpeg)

If you’re staying in [Fisherman’s Wharf](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1432%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=MY1ZpGwZ54AETONkhz2ZH&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), get ready for tourist-central vibes. Think tons of souvenir shops, big-chain stores, and seafood stalls where you can grab a quick bite from the bay. They **do** make bread bowls here in the shape of animals so that’s a plus at least.

[Fisherman’s Wharf](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1432%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=qkj0D40raN-KIvx7k2-uv&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is obviously not where the locals hang, but it’s the best spot if you want to be close to [Pier 39](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D11165%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=5U6iZe5zj4jkohc5EOQjw&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), [Ghirardelli Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17265%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=Fmlq6DbS551PU9xy2Aad3&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), and the adorable sea lions at Aquatic Park.

Just be warned that it’s a bit chaotic but there’s a great selection of hotels and no shortage of things to do and see if you’re into the full SF tourist experience.

### Where to stay in San Francisco’s Fisherman’s Wharf: Top boutique hotel picks

- [Hotel Caza Fisherman’s Wharf —](https://tripadvisor.tpk.lu/sLXkmVuC?trs=299090&journey_id=Oheax9_mj644AKrYGSI0J&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_short&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") A laid-back stay in Fisherman’s Wharf, Hotel Caza mixes modern rooms with a fun, family-friendly vibe. You’re steps from the waterfront, with easy access to Pier 39, Ghirardelli Square, and cable cars. It’s simple, comfortable, and perfectly located if you want to be in the heart of the action. ### Things to do in Fisherman’s Wharf

![](https://i.imgur.com/iQTUxf1.jpeg)

Like I mentioned earlier, Fisherman’s Wharf is all about the touristy fun so you can’t be mad about it if you’re planning to stay here.

You’ve got the classic [Pier 39](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D11165%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=o4xZzEIEII1xhs5UuODs2&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) with its candy shops and sea lions. Yes, the sea lions are a must-see. And a bunch of fresh seafood joints to hit up (get that clam chowder in a turtle-shaped sourdough bowl).

Don’t forget Ghirardelli Square for chocolate and a make-your-own ice cream sundae, or hop on a boat to check out [Alcatraz](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Falcatraz-l535%2F&trs=299090&journey_id=bne3uorwzwAS7oUdrQJ6O&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner ""). Even as a local, I’ll head to [Alcatraz](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Falcatraz-l535%2F&trs=299090&journey_id=IVF-ptQCpx-mVaheZPEw3&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") at least once every couple years when I’m showing people around. It’s touristy but also the history is fascinating.

There’s also a really [fun night tour of Alcatraz](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fsan-francisco-l61%2Fsan-francisco-alcatraz-ticket-ferry-self-guided-app-t822893%2F%3Franking_uuid%3D6a30ea38-65a3-4b21-8bd8-289e4d634fc8&trs=299090&journey_id=rjNiTZJUuN2zvsAkmVFXw&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") where you get to visit the prison at night. It’s a bit creepy but totally worth it. Plus, the views of the city from across the way are STUNNING, making it one of the safest places to stay in San Francisco for a memorable experience.

**Main Takeaway**: [Fisherman’s Wharf](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1432%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=Pg1uCb_4yOuAzua5pHiIT&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is a great place to stay if you don’t mind being in tourist central. It’s known to be safe, and the area is packed with souvenir shops, local attractions, and top-rated seafood 🦀

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: Financial District (FIDI)

![](https://i.imgur.com/mhOWEPh.jpeg)

This area’s mostly for my business travelers and/or conference folks but there are some incredible hotels in downtown San Francisco that I would totally stay in even if you’re not traveling for work. [FIDI](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D12560860%26dest_type%3Dhotel&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=jiQET05eB6s2Cw_wkekDV&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is San Francisco’s main financial district but it also extends into parts of [Soma](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D4065499%26dest_type%3Dhotel&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=IutEjGaXssG4u3EPuDzib&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) (south of [Market street](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17254%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=AbradJxH6-AqkN3LUBysU&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F)) and [The Embarcadero](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a8932%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=0kO86wI5mWGw3m9lX1d6u&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) (the main road along the water).

Similar to most cities, this area is commonly referred to as “downtown SF” 🙂

### Things to do in Financial District (FIDI)

![](https://i.imgur.com/mLMhfXC.jpeg)

Surprisingly FIDI isn’t just for business travelers. It’s got some serious personality and some beautiful cityscapes once you find the right spots. You’ve got the [Transamerica Pyramid](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=4456&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FAttraction_Review-g60713-d144408-Reviews-Transamerica_Pyramid-San_Francisco_California.html&trs=299090&journey_id=Pm2XctO13HslR1B4pMCrs&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") looming overhead, which is one of San Francisco’s most recognizable landmarks.

Completed in 1972, this triangle-shaped building was once the tallest in the city and still stands as a symbol of modern architecture. While you can’t exactly wander up to the top (unless you’re lucky enough to work there), the building’s unique shape and striking presence make it a must-see from almost every corner of downtown.

Just down the road, you’ve got the [SFMOMA](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=108&marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fsan-francisco-l61%2Fentry-tickets-san-francisco-museum-of-modern-art-sfmoma-t411332%2F%3Fcurrency%3DUSD%26psrc%3Dpartner_api&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=dGnF2ZzRqbdn4xcTDqVjX&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) museum and the historic [Ferry Building](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17253%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=OlziGV3wgm8RIm04rrV6x&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) for delicious eats.

The [Ferry Building](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=4456&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FAttraction_Review-g60713-d103851-Reviews-Ferry_Building_Marketplace-San_Francisco_California.html&trs=299090&journey_id=T6SxNeqnkgh8-dBBDbRCN&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") is a foodie paradise and one of San Francisco’s best spots for local eats, waterfront views, and a little history. Originally built in 1898 as the city’s main transportation hub, it’s now home to the Ferry Building Marketplace, where you’ll find everything from artisanal cheese at Cowgirl Creamery to fresh oysters at Hog Island Oyster Co 🦪

And hey, if you’re feeling fancy, you can always hit up [Verjus](https://www.verjuscave.com/ "") or [San Francisco Wine Society](https://www.sanfranciscowinesociety.com/ "") — two of my favorite wine bars downtown 🍷

**Main Takeaway**: If you’re looking for a central, well-connected place to stay in San Francisco, the [Financial District](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1620%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=sYcaMduZu416l-DRhc5kV&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) is a solid pick. Especially for business travelers or those who love being near top restaurants, the [Ferry Building](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17253%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=qZfEQiX54DNFlMdqs65HF&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), and easy transit options like BART and MUNI. It’s not the most “neighborhood-y” area, but it’s clean, safe, and considered one of the safest places to stay in San Francisco, with easy walking access to [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=nNKLAVNifZYyKbCml7X1d&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), [Chinatown](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1431%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=Xl_DL03_OzKZbeiLVd1wJ&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), and the [Embarcadero](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a8932%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=yWwmD0ad_7wGXKFexsfyg&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F).

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: The Richmond District

![](https://i.imgur.com/EVeYcVB.jpeg)

Annndddd last but not least — the beautiful, lovely, and oh so quiet San Francisco’s [Richmond District](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1424%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=P6gRvUZSniHmp81noiY8Y&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F)!

This neighborhood is where fog meets flavor, packed with some of the city’s best dim sum, cozy cafes, and shockingly good Russian bakeries (yes, you need a piroshki).

You’re a short stroll from [Golden Gate Park](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17258%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=haIQBVCMNQkZyoZ9qkeTc&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), [the Presidio](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a16137%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=MFT6kVJEG2MkkLUsyLdE8&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), and [Ocean Beach](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a8931%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=c4M8vGCjVTNcycILvnoRD&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), so whether you’re into museums, scenic hikes, or just staring dramatically at the Pacific, you’re covered.

Bonus: it’s waaaaay quieter than downtown, and you won’t have to dodge a million pigeons or robot taxis getting stuck on the streets.

### Where to stay in San Francisco’s Richmond District: Top vacation rental picks

There truly aren’t any hotels in The Richmond — that’s how residential it is. But there are some amazing gems on [Airbnb](https://www.airbnb.com/s/Richmond-District--San-Francisco--CA--USA/homes?refinement_paths%5B%5D=%2Fhomes&flexible_trip_lengths%5B%5D=one_week&monthly_start_date=2025-03-01&monthly_length=3&monthly_end_date=2025-06-01&price_filter_input_type=2&channel=EXPLORE&query=Richmond%20District%2C%20San%20Francisco%2C%20CA&place_id=ChIJK8HVABGHhYARPbkNZPtKm9E&date_picker_type=calendar&source=structured_search_input_header&search_type=user_map_move&search_mode=regular_search&price_filter_num_nights=5&ne_lat=37.79912721779363&ne_lng=-122.46639788803833&sw_lat=37.74566450094218&sw_lng=-122.49946211196169&zoom=14.359489793060387&zoom_level=14.359489793060387&search_by_map=true "") and [VRBO](https://vrbo.stay22.com/discoveroverthere/m0PcEI0r7E "") so I definitely recommend checking out both platforms for a quiet stay in a lovely Victorian.

![](https://i.imgur.com/6ku0Wyt.png)

### Things to do in the Richmond

The Richmond District is like your local San Francisco secret, packed with a little something for everyone.

Start with a buttery croissant from [Arsicault Bakery,](https://arsicault-bakery.com/ "") voted #1 croissant in San Francisco 🥐

After that, head over to [Golden Gate Park](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17258%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=GkRSwSrKRSkn1WAupZJcd&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) to get your nature fix. Whether it’s wandering through the [Japanese Tea Garden](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17284%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=gnjYM54ZT3hA1jAAeQgDn&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), geeking out at the [California Academy of Sciences](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=108&marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fcalifornia-academy-of-sciences-l5125%2Fskip-the-line-california-academy-of-sciences-entrance-t8481%2F%3Fcurrency%3DUSD%26psrc%3Dpartner_api&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=o28q1rM8PRV2DPQ9rkBbK&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), or soaking in art at the [de Young Museum](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Ftours%2FSan-Francisco%2Fde-Young-Museum-Admission%2Fd651-5959DEYOUNG%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=AoiuRZFTB6QpJby92ARA_&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F).

Not enough fresh air? Hit up the [Presidio](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D11308%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=H4a0alAFPcSKs3Kv3hyte&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) for killer views of the [Golden Gate Bridge](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a1063%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=4txFKGDHwZUEQHZywZLdH&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) or chill at [Baker Beach](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D168146%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=xzdMWeik9g57WnnRriizM&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). Oh, and the food scene? From next-level dim sum to Russian pastries, your taste buds are in for a treat.

I probably Doordash Asian food from the Richmond at least once a week. My absolute favorites are [B-Star](https://www.bstarbar.com/ "") (Burmese), [Mamahuhu](https://eatmamahuhu.com/ "")(Chinese), and [Kowloon Tong Dessert Cafe](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=4456&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FRestaurant_Review-g60713-d3915791-Reviews-Kowloon_Tong_Dessert_Cafe-San_Francisco_California.html&trs=299090&journey_id=OBeoSXK01UuSbZOalBEhH&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") (HK style dessert).

**Main Takeaway:** Staying in the Richmond means getting the perfect mix of local charm and easy access to nature. Think quiet streets, cozy spots, and quick trips to [Golden Gate Park](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17258%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=asBTPFIToemiVbnPvFddq&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) and the coast. It’s also one of the safest places to stay in San Francisco, making it the ideal base for those who want to explore the city without the tourist crowds.

## San Francisco FAQ

Here are some commonly asked questions for first time visitors to San Francisco, California ☀️

![](https://i.imgur.com/hg9WiXP.jpeg)

### What areas should I avoid?

San Francisco is an incredible city, but like any major metro, there are a few areas you’ll want to steer clear of — mainly the **[Tenderloin](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D2128%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=3CTpALw0aniOT46gTK28m&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F)** and the stretch of **[SoMa](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=104&marker=522542&p=2854&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.agoda.com%2Fsearch%3Fasq%3Du2qcKLxwzRU5NDuxJ0kOF3T91go8JoYYMxAgy8FkBH1BN0lGAtYH25sdXoy34qb9eEsQWZsoSSHE3njZoVXTqK%252Bo4MSnEA%252FMyeCu%252BzzlJex%252FsxJxt6cnX%252BFI4%252Fq5SldOikrSP3cx4715NAYXt0MMqe%252F%252FsCZ5iXDKU0Picl3lP83amqOIM6BiyvWEp3YpzMZxMmg4DCCO8vgy22FxJvZZEMaEH2QqG1%252FO5HV31AKaQl0%253D%26hotel%3D42069025%26selectedproperty%3D42069025%26tick%3D639007525200&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=3GL0X04t2n-hz_NOxYb_h&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) between 6th and 10th Street**.

These areas have higher crime rates, open-air drug use, and generally aren’t the best for walking around, especially at night.

areas to avoid SF - Google My Maps

The good news? SF is mostly made up of safe, walkable neighborhoods, and my guide focuses on the safest places to stay in San Francisco, steering you clear of any areas you’ll want to avoid.

### Do I need to rent a car in San Francisco?

![](https://i.imgur.com/rsWKxIO.jpeg)

[Renting a car](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3555&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.discovercars.com%2Fusa-california%2Fsan-francisco%2Fsfo&trs=299090&journey_id=oxIvhCWtKd95ukVvFRClw&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") in San Francisco can sometimes be more of a hassle than a help. So I think it depends on whether or not you are visiting areas outside of the city. I’d definitely recommend it if you’re wanting to spend a couple days in wine country or drive down the coast to Monterey, Carmel, [Big Sur](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a10674%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=CJNI0Xq7SOyrWCXQJV_Ry&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), etc.

Then yes! Definitely [rent a car](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3555&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.discovercars.com%2Fusa-california%2Fsan-francisco%2Fsfo&trs=299090&journey_id=9CmUApdKNIAPVROjDgZCf&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") 🚘

But if you’re only planning on visiting San Francisco and/or seeing its immediate surrounding areas, then NO. I don’t think you will need or should rent a car. Since between expensive parking, confusing street signs, and the city’s (in)famous hills, you’re usually better off using public transit or uber/lyft/waymo.

But if you do [rent a car](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3555&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.discovercars.com%2Fusa-california%2Fsan-francisco%2Fsfo&trs=299090&journey_id=P_U6KhMOO8Bpt1_T3LD_l&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner ""), just remember **one golden rule: never leave anything in the car.**

Car break-ins are unfortunately common, and thieves don’t discriminate. If they see a bag, jacket, or even an empty box, they’ll smash and grab.

So, if you must drive, keep the car completely empty when parked.

### What’s the best way to get around San Francisco?

Getting around San Francisco is a breeze if you know your options. And luckily for us, we have so many different methods of public transportation to get around. Including driver-less vehicles 🤖🚘

I guess we are at the forefront of technology so it makes sense.

- **Walking** – SF is a super walkable city (minus the hills), and most major attractions are within a few miles of each other
- **Muni (Buses & Light Rail)** – The cheapest way to get around, Muni covers the entire city with buses and streetcars. Just download the MuniMobile app for easy payment
- **Rideshares (Uber/Lyft/Waymo)** – Great for avoiding hills and late-night travel when public transit is less frequent
- **Biking & Scooters** – Rent a **Bay Wheels** bike or **Lime scooter** to cruise along the waterfront or through Golden Gate Park
- **Cable Cars**– A must-do at least once! The Powell-Hyde and Powell-Mason lines are the most scenic
- **Ferries** – Heading to Sausalito or Alcatraz? The ferry is the way to go, with stunning views of the bay
- **BART (Bay Area Rapid Transit)** – Best for getting to/from the airport or hopping between SF and the East Bay

### How long do you recommend staying in San Francisco?

I think 3-4 days is the perfect amount of time to experience most of what San Francisco has to offer. For a complete itinerary, check out my guide on [how to spend 3 unforgettable days in San Francisco (w/ sample itinerary)](https://discoveroverthere.com/3-day-san-francisco-itinerary/ "").

I also created this [local’s 3-day guide on Thatch](https://www.thatch.co/guide/kc5qnoxv33mh/edit "") that has all of my favorite spots pinned on a map 🗺️

## Safest Areas to Stay in San Francisco: Final Thoughts

![](https://i.imgur.com/YhUVYnz.jpeg)

So, here’s the deal: San Francisco is a total gem, and there’s no reason to let the mainstream media scare you off. The city is packed with safe, vibrant, and fun neighborhoods that easily make it one of the safest places to stay in San Francisco!

Whether you’re crashing in [Union Square](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1735%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=OSRXOkB8VbKI4AfVB7BDO&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), soaking in the Marina girlie (or guy) vibes, or living your best life in [Nob Hill](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D1436%26dest_type%3Ddistrict&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=Dgw2ial_fTEu1agtH3mqR&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F). There’s always something to do, from exploring [Fort Mason](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=84&marker=522542&p=2076&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fsearchresults.en-gb.html%3Fdest_id%3D17268%26dest_type%3Dlandmark&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=ALokyxz7GM5I7OS-fYzV1&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F) to checking out iconic spots like the [Golden Gate Bridge](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=47&marker=522542&p=1922&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.viator.com%2Fx-attractions%2Fy%2Fd0-a1063%3Fapi_version%3D2.0&trs=299090&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&install_type=am_partner_content&product_type=emerald&journey_id=a5jqyuKM8Euvjqc3eCScL&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F), or indulging in insane food🍴

Sure, no place is perfect, but with a little insider knowledge, you’ll find that San Francisco is full of welcoming areas to stay, play, and eat your heart out.

Don’t overthink it. San Francisco is a fabulous, safe area to visit, and you’re going to love it 🌁

Look, I know San Francisco gets a bad rap these days, but let me set the record straight — this city is absolutely **_stunning_.** I personally grew up in the Bay Area and have lived in San Francisco for the last decade. Yet, I continue to be obsessed with our pastel-colored Victorians, the cable cars chugging along California street, and the views of the Golden Gate bridge at sunset from Crissy Field. If you ignore the overly negative image the media loves to push, then you’ll soon understand why **thousands** of people fall head over heels for SF every year 🌁

Yes, just like any major city, we have our rough areas, but the “doomloop” headlines don’t tell the full story. **The reality?** We’re a buzzing, innovative city with some of the cutest boutique hotels and the most charming neighborhoods. So trust me, you’ll have plenty of great options when deciding where to stay in San Francisco.

## Breakdown of San Francisco Neighborhoods

![](https://i.imgur.com/MPZSeYX.jpeg)

[San Francisco](https://emrldtp.com/re?campaign_id=594&marker=522542&p=8645&trs=299090&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.expedia.com%2FHotel-Search%3Fadults%3D2%26afflid%3D1100lAdhTYT4%26clickref%3D1100lAdhTYT4%26my_ad%3DAFF.US.DIRECT.PHG.1011l45458.0%26numRoom%3D1%26ref_id%3D1100lAdhTYT4%26regionId%3D3132&product_type=linkswitcher&journey_id=AQqCWDmxuEl8_H6TbWXkx&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&install_type=partner ""), located on the northern tip of California’s San Francisco Peninsula, is a vibrant city known for its stunning views, classic landmarks, and rich history. Spanning just 7 miles by 7 miles, it’s also one of the most compact major cities in the U.S.

Ps. SF is literally nicknamed [7×7](https://www.7x7.com/ "") because of how small our city dimensions are.

San Francisco’s neighborhoods are as diverse as the people who live here, and trust me, there’s a spot for everyone. The Marina and Pacific Heights are your go-to for stunning views and chic dining, while Nob Hill and Russian Hill serve up a little old-school charm with those iconic, sweeping panoramas. And hills 🥵

If you’re in the mood for classic tourist fun, head over to Fisherman’s Wharf for seafood, shopping, and all the sights. Union Square’s got your back for shopping and art, while the Financial District (FiDi) pulses with business energy.

Richmond and Sunset? A quieter, more laid-back vibe with cozy restaurants and parks to relax in. Many of these neighborhoods fall under the safest areas in San Francisco to stay, making your visit both fun and worry-free. Whether you’re looking for charm, views, or convenience, the safest areas in San Francisco to stay offer something for every kind of traveler. So stick with me, and I’ll take you through each one — neighborhood by neighborhood!

## Where to Stay in San Francisco

Now that you’ve got a feel for how big the city is and how things are laid out, let’s get into the safest areas to stay while visiting San Francisco! You won’t need a car if you’re staying in these areas, although it never hurts [to rent one](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3555&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.discovercars.com%2F&trs=299090&journey_id=cN0fIw1PLPr8S-6BO19Be&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") if you want to go beyond the city.

Aka like maybe up to [wine country](https://discoveroverthere.com/category/destinations/north-america/california/wine-country/ "") or down the coast for a day 🍷🌊

## Where to Stay in San Francisco: The Marina

![](https://i.imgur.com/LK7eeEX.jpeg)

I know, I know. Every guidebook and travel blog will probably tell you to stay in Union Square. But let me let you in on a little secret: the Marina District is where it’s _really_ at.

I actually lived here for over five years before my fiancé and I made the move to Nob Hill, so I’m speaking from experience when I say it’s hands down the best neighborhood in San Francisco.

From stunning views of the [Golden Gate](https://emrldtp.com/re?marker=522542&p=3965&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.getyourguide.com%2Fsan-francisco-l61%2F&trs=299090&journey_id=ORDjjY5HHpjm_fmoXTk2x&trace_id=Zz25306174fc714d908c75f46-522542&promo_kind=tp_other&page_url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscoveroverthere.com%2Fwhere-to-stay-in-san-francisco%2F&product_type=tp_manual&install_type=partner "") to charming boutiques, fitness studios, and top-notch dining, it’s got the perfect mix of everything.

Plus, it’s one of the safest areas in San Francisco to stay. Whether you’re walking around at night or grabbing coffee in the morning, you’ll feel totally at ease. The safest areas when deciding where to stay in San Francisco aren’t just secure, they’re also full of character. The Marina is a perfect example, with charm, walkability, and classic SF vibes.

Trust me, if you’re looking for a spot to stay that’s both lively and secure, the Marina’s got you covered.
